msg:Yancheng Marriott Hotel is really bad, with poor service, management and hygiene. It is not comparable to the InterContinental Hotel in Yancheng.
In order to reunite with my family during the Spring Festival, I placed an order on the Ctrip platform two months ago and booked 5 rooms at the Yancheng Marriott Hotel for two nights. On the day of check-in, the front desk lady went around and around to check in for more than half an hour. What's more disgusting is that the 5 rooms of one order were deliberately arranged on 5 different floors. When I raised an objection, the manager on duty replied: Some people don't want to be arranged on the same floor!
The poor hygiene is beyond description. A five-star hotel can actually see spider webs and living things in the room. It's disgusting! Is this the hygiene standard of a 5-star hotel? It feels that it is not as good as a chain hotel. The feedback to the hotel is also inconclusive. Except for a perfunctory apology, there is no attitude and practical measures to solve the problem...
The quality of the Marriott Group has been discredited by the Yancheng Marriott Hotel, and it is not ruled out that the relevant personnel of the hotel want to deliberately mess up the Marriott brand.
